(default settings should work for Nikon cameras and a few others)\r\n- Tap 'connect' to establish PTP/IP connection to your camera\r\n\r\n\r\nSetup with cameras that connects to an existing network:\r\n\r\n- Turn on camera's Wi-Fi networking and specify an existing wireless access point to connect to.
